;;; Test Implication Direct Introduction DTL Rule
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta)

% DEBUG:   eval('&self',['import!','&self','ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta'],OUT).

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/dependent-types/ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/dependent-types/ImplicationDirectIntroductionDTL.metta')
;;; MeTTa port of the Implication Direct Introduction PLN rule, encoded
;;; as dependent types, i.e. propositions as types.
;;;
;;; See ImplicationDirectIntroductionEntail.metta for more detail on a
;;; pseudo formal description.
;;;
;;; In the case of dependent types, inference rules are constructors of
;;; the propositions to be proven.  Then a proof is an tree composed of
;;; calls of such constructors.
;;;
;;; For instance assuming two inference rules
;;;
;;; ImplicationDirectIntroduction (IDI, for short)
;;; Deduction (DED, for short)
;;;
;;; The following inference tree
;;;
;;; ...            ...
;;; -----(IDI)     -----(IDI)
;;; P → Q          Q → R
;;; ---------------------(DED)
;;;         P → R
;;;
;;; is represented by the following MeTTa expression
;;;
;;; (Deduction
;;;    (ImplicationDirectIntroduction ...)
;;;    (ImplicationDirectIntroduction ...))
;;;
;;; where the premises of ImplicationDirectIntroduction are left
;;; undefined for now.
;;;
;;; How such propositions as types can be defined still remains to be
;;; determined but ideally it may look something like
;;;
;;; (: Deduction
;;;    (-> (≞ (→ $P $Q) $TV1)
;;;        (≞ (→ $Q $R) $TV2)
;;;        (≞ (→ $P $R) (deduction-formula $TV1 $TV2))))
;;;
;;; where ≞, → are dependent types, and formula is just a regular metta
;;; function.
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta")

% DEBUG:   eval('&self',['import!','&self','../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta'],OUT).

    -->(1,eval('&self',['import!','&self','../common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta'],RET),depth(0))
%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/EvidentialTruthValue.metta')

    (> $X $Y) $X $Y))

(: STV 
  (-> Number Number TruthValue))

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
(: count->confidence 
  (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]]])
(= 
  (count->confidence $Cnt) 
  (/ $Cnt 
    (+ $Cnt 
      (lookahead))))


;;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;;
;;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
(: confidence->count 
  (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]]])
(= 
  (confidence->count $Conf) 
  (if 
    (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
    (max-count) 
    (/ 
      (* $Conf 
        (lookahead)) 
      (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;;; Increment the negative count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count without incrementing the positive
;;; count.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
(: inc-neg-count 
  (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-neg-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,Pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
(= 
  (inc-neg-count 
    (STV $S $C)) 
  (let* 
    ( ($Tot_cnt 
        (confidence->count $C)) 
      ($Pos_cnt 
        (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
      ($New_tot_cnt 
        (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
    (STV 
      (/ $Pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
      (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Increment the positive count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count and its positive count.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
(: inc-pos-count 
  (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-pos-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_pos_cnt,[+,Pos_cnt,1]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,New_pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
(= 
  (inc-pos-count 
    (STV $S $C)) 
  (let* 
    ( ($Tot_cnt 
        (confidence->count $C)) 
      ($Pos_cnt 
        (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
      ($New_pos_cnt 
        (+ $Pos_cnt 1)) 
      ($New_tot_cnt 
        (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
    (STV 
      (/ $New_pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
      (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: mode 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr])
(= 
  (mode 
    (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;;; be supported at the moment).
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: count 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count']])
(= 
  (count 
    (Bl $_)) 
  (max-count))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count']])
(= 
  (count 
    (Pr $_)) 
  (max-count))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf]])
(= 
  (count 
    (STV $_ $Conf)) 
  (confidence->count $Conf))


;;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;;; notion of confidence, such as STV, the formula to convert a count
;;; into confidence is as follows
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: confidence 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: pos-count

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['pos-count',Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]]])
(= 
  (pos-count $Tv) 
  (* 
    (mode $Tv) 
    (count $Tv)))

;;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Rule Definition ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; All rules are implemented as constructors of propositions encoded
;;; as types.
;;; To deal with an abritrary number of pieces of evidence the rule is
;;; defined inductively.
;;; Base case (one piece of evidence):
;;;
;;; (p a) = True
;;; (q a) = qa
;;; â¢
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: a â) tv)
;;;
;;; where tv is calculated according to the direct introduction
;;; formula.  Note that we don't bother to take into account pieces of
;;; evidence that is not True on (p a), because it has no impact on the
;;; resulting truth value otherwise.
;;;
;;; To avoid prematurely reducing (p a) = pa to pa = pa, the following
;;; representation is used instead
;;;
;;; (â· p a pa)
;;;
;;; which can be read as "under p, the image of a is pa".
;;;
;;; â· is essentially the Atomese equivalent of ExecutionLink.  It has
;;; description: IMAGE OF, hexadecimal code: 0x22B7, unicode-math code:
;;; \imageof and latex code: \multimapdotbothB.
;;; Formula for the inductive Implication Direct Introduction rule.
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta")

% DEBUG:   eval('&self',['import!','&self','../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta'],OUT).

    -->(7,eval('&self',['import!','&self','../truthvalue/TruthValue.metta'],RET),depth(0))
%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/TruthValue.metta.answers',
%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/baseline_compat/hyperon-pln_metta/common/truthvalue/TruthValue.metta')

;;; evidence.  Base case, meaning there is only one piece of evidence.
;;; Truth value type definition
;;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../Num.metta")

;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;;; Define max
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
(: max 
  (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y]])
(= 
  (max $X $Y) 
  (if 
    (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Define min
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
(: min 
  (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y]])
(= 
  (min $X $Y) 
  (if 
    (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
(: clamp 
  (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]]])
(= 
  (clamp $X $L $U) 
  (max $L 
    (min $U $X)))


;;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
(: abs 
  (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X]])
(= 
  (abs $X) 
  (if 
    (< $X 0) 
    (* -1 $X) $X))


;;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
(: <= 
  (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]]])
(= 
  (<= $X $Y) 
  (or 
    (< $X $Y) 
    (== $X $Y)))


;;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
(: >= 
  (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]]])
(= 
  (>= $X $Y) 
  (or 
    (> $X $Y) 
    (== $X $Y)))


;;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
(: approxEq 
  (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon]])
(= 
  (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
  (<= 
    (abs 
      (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))


;;; Define Nat
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'Nat','Type'])
(: Nat Type)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'Z','Nat'])
(: Z Nat)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'S',[->,'Nat','Nat']])
(: S 
  (-> Nat Nat))


;;; Define cast functions between Nat and Number
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNumber,[->,'Number','Nat']])
(: fromNumber 
  (-> Number Nat))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNumber,N],[if,[<=,N,0],'Z',['S',[fromNumber,[-,N,1]]]]])
(= 
  (fromNumber $N) 
  (if 
    (<= $N 0) Z 
    (S 
      (fromNumber 
        (- $N 1)))))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,fromNat,[->,'Nat','Number']])
(: fromNat 
  (-> Nat Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNat,'Z'],0])
(= 
  (fromNat Z) 0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[fromNat,['S',K]],[+,1,[fromNat,K]]])
(= 
  (fromNat 
    (S $K)) 
  (+ 1 
    (fromNat $K)))


;;; Define a generic less than operator, â©», for Nat.  < cannot be used
;;; because it is a built-in, its type is hardwired and cannot be
;;; overloaded.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'â©»',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])
(: â©» 
  (-> Nat Nat Bool))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',_,'Z'],'False'])
(= 
  (â©» $_ Z) False)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»','Z',['S',_]],'True'])
(= 
  (â©» Z 
    (S $_)) True)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',['S',X],['S',Y]],['â©»',X,Y]])
(= 
  (â©» 
    (S $X) 
    (S $Y)) 
  (â©» $X $Y))


;;; Overload â©» for Number.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'â©»',[->,'Number','Number','Bool']])
(: â©» 
  (-> Number Number Bool))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['â©»',X,Y],[<,X,Y]])
(= 
  (â©» $X $Y) 
  (< $X $Y))


;;; Return the ceiling of a non negative number.  If the number is
;;; negative it returns 1.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,ceil,[->,'Number','Number']])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[ceil,N],[fromNat,[fromNumber,N]]])
(= 
  (ceil $N) 
  (fromNat 
    (fromNumber $N)))


;;; Convert Number to Bool.  Anything above 0 converts to True.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'number->bool',[->,'Number','Bool']])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['number->bool',X],[<,0,X]])
(= 
  (number->bool $X) 
  (< 0 $X))


;;; Convert Bool to Number.  False converts to 0, True converts to 1.

(= 
  (bool->number False) 0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['bool->number','True'],1])
(= 
  (bool->number True) 1)

;;; If x â y then (S x) â (S y)

      (â $X $Y)

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])

  (-> Number Number TruthValue))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-alpha',[->,'Number']])
(: prior-alpha

;;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
(: count->confidence 
  (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]]])
(= 
  (count->confidence $Cnt) 
  (/ $Cnt 
    (+ $Cnt 
      (lookahead))))


;;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;;
;;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
(: confidence->count 
  (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]]])
(= 
  (confidence->count $Conf) 
  (if 
    (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
    (max-count) 
    (/ 
      (* $Conf 
        (lookahead)) 
      (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;;; Increment the negative count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count without incrementing the positive
;;; count.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
(: inc-neg-count 
  (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-neg-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,Pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
(= 
  (inc-neg-count 
    (STV $S $C)) 
  (let* 
    ( ($Tot_cnt 
        (confidence->count $C)) 
      ($Pos_cnt 
        (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
      ($New_tot_cnt 
        (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
    (STV 
      (/ $Pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
      (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Increment the positive count of a given truth value, by
;;; incrementing its total count and its positive count.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
(: inc-pos-count 
  (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['inc-pos-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_pos_cnt,[+,Pos_cnt,1]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,New_pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]]])
(= 
  (inc-pos-count 
    (STV $S $C)) 
  (let* 
    ( ($Tot_cnt 
        (confidence->count $C)) 
      ($Pos_cnt 
        (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
      ($New_pos_cnt 
        (+ $Pos_cnt 1)) 
      ($New_tot_cnt 
        (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
    (STV 
      (/ $New_pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
      (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: mode 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr])
(= 
  (mode 
    (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr])
(= 
  (mode 
    (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;;; be supported at the moment).
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: count 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count']])
(= 
  (count 
    (Bl $_)) 
  (max-count))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count']])
(= 
  (count 
    (Pr $_)) 
  (max-count))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf]])
(= 
  (count 
    (STV $_ $Conf)) 
  (confidence->count $Conf))


;;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;;; notion of confidence, such as STV, the formula to convert a count
;;; into confidence is as follows
;;;
;;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: confidence 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf])
(= 
  (confidence 
    (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: pos-count 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['pos-count',Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]]])
(= 
  (pos-count $Tv) 
  (* 
    (mode $Tv) 
    (count $Tv)))


;;; Return the negative count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
(: neg-count 
  (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['neg-count',Tv],[*,[-,1,[mode,Tv]],[count,Tv]]])
(= 
  (neg-count $Tv) 
  (* 
    (- 1 
      (mode $Tv)) 
    (count $Tv)))


;;; Return the posterior alpha of a truth value
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-alpha',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])

;;; Return the posterior beta of a truth value
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-beta',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])

    (prior-beta)

;;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not

;;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a

(= 
  (mean 
    (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[mean,['STV',Pr,Conf]],['let*',[[A,['post-alpha',['STV',Pr,Conf]]],[B,['post-beta',['STV',Pr,Conf]]]],[/,A,[+,A,B]]]])
(= 
  (mean 
    (STV $Pr $Conf))

    ( ($A 
        (post-alpha 
          (STV $Pr $Conf))) 
      ($B 
        (post-beta 
          (STV $Pr $Conf)))) 
    (/ $A 
      (+ $A $B))))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'implication-direct-introduction-base-rule',[->,'Atom']])

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,['implication-direct-introduction-base-rule'],[:,'IDIBase',[->,['â\x8A\·',P,A,'True'],['â\x8A\·',Q,A,Qa],['â\x89\\x9E\',['â\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',[::,A,'â\x88\\x85\'],['direct-introduction-base-formula',Qa]]]]]])

    (->

;;; Recursive step (more than one piece of evidence):
;;;
;;; (p a) = True
;;; (q a) = qa
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: h t) pqtv)
;;; h < a
;;; â¢
;;; pâq â (ETV (:: a (:: h t)) tv)
;;;
;;; where tv is calculated using the direct introduction formula.  Note
;;; that we don't bother to take into account pieces of evidence that
;;; is not True on (p a), because it has no impact on the resulting
;;; truth value otherwise.
;;;
;;; To avoid prematurely reducing (p a) = pa to pa = pa, the following
;;; representation is used instead
;;;
;;; (â· p a pa)
;;;
;;; which can be read as "under p, the image of a is pa".
;;;
;;; For a similar reason, the premise h < a is represented as
;;;
;;; h â a
;;;
;;; â is the axiomatized version of <.  It is defined in Num.metta.
;;; The box around the less than sign is here to manifest its
;;; axiomatic, as opposed to computational, nature.  It has
;;; description: APL FUNCTIONAL SYMBOL QUAD LESS-THAN and hexadecimal
;;; code: 0x2343.
;;;
;;; The h â a premise is there to garanty that evidence is not double
;;; counted.
;;;
;;; Historical note: initially the premise
;;;
;;; h â a
;;;
;;; was replaced by
;;;
;;; a â (:: h t)
;;;
;;; But then it was realized that it is far more efficient to enforce
;;; the order in which evidence can be pilled up, than to prove that a
;;; new piece of evidence does not belongs to an existing evidence set.
;;; And now you know why time is the way it is.
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,'implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule',[->,'Atom']])
(: implication-direct-introduction-recursive-rule 
  (-> Atom))

;;; !(import! &self Unify.metta)
;;; Enumerate all programs up to a given depth that are consistent with
;;; the query, using the given axiom non-deterministic functions and rules.
;;;
;;; The arguments are:
;;;
;;; $query: an Atom under the form (: TERM TYPE).  The atom may contain
;;;         free variables within TERM and TYPE to form various sort of
;;;         queries, such as:
;;;         1. Backward chaining: (: $term (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;;         2. Forward chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) $type)
;;;         3. Mixed chaining: (: ($rule $premise AXIOM) (Inheritance $x Mammal))
;;;         4. Type checking: (: TERM TYPE)
;;;         5. Type inference: (: TERM $type)
;;;
;;; $kb: a nullary function to axiom, to non-deterministically pick up
;;;      an axiom.  An axiom is an Atom of the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;;
;;; $rb: a nullary function to rule, to non-deterministically pick up a
;;;      rule.  A rule is a function mapping premises to conclusion,
;;;      where premises and conclusion have the form (: TERM TYPE).
;;;
;;; $depth: a Nat representing the maximum depth of the generated
;;;         programs.
;;;
;;; TODO: recurse over curried rules instead of duplicating code over
;;; tuples.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;;; Define max
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
(: max 
  (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y]])
(= 
  (max $X $Y) 
  (if 
    (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Define min
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
(: min 
  (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y]])
(= 
  (min $X $Y) 
  (if 
    (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
(: clamp 
  (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]]])
(= 
  (clamp $X $L $U) 
  (max $L 
    (min $U $X)))


;;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
(: abs 
  (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[=,[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X]])
(= 
  (abs $X) 
  (if 
    (< $X 0) 
    (* -1 $X) $X))


;;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
(: <= 
  (-> $A $A Bool))

  ; Action: load=asserted_metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
